<h2 id="anchor-4">4. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-elm-basics-122047" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Elm Basics (Jesse Warden)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85501" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Elm-Basics-Jesse-Warden.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Elm-Basics-Jesse-Warden.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Elm-Basics-Jesse-Warden-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-Elm-Basics-Jesse-Warden-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-elm-basics-122047" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Elm Basics</a> is a <b>free</b> short crash course where you’ll build a working Elm application in less than an hour with VSCode and Node.js. It covers less of the theoretical concepts and more on getting you started.</p>
<p>You should have some experience in any programming language to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll begin this course by setting up Elm in VSCode and its necessary plugins and tools, such as the REPL, make, and init. Then, after creating the source JSON file, you’ll initialize a local web development server and begin writing your first Elm application.</p>
<p>You’ll go over the basic structure of an Elm application, which consists of the main function as well as the Elm architecture of Model-View-Update. The three-part architecture requires an initial value of the model, a view function to represent the model on the screen and an update method to handle the changes to the data. Next, you’ll learn how to handle user input in the case of text forms or buttons, and trigger an event to send a message to the model and request an update to the model. You’ll also understand how to use the Maybe type to handle the possibility of errors when parsing user input.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 1 hour long. You’ll learn by watching the series of instructional videos and following along with the instructor as he demonstrates the ins-and-outs of developing an Elm application.</p>

</ul>

<h2 id="anchor-5">5. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-an-introduction-to-elm-122048" target="_blank" rel="noopener">An Introduction to Elm (elm-lang.org)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85502" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-An-Introduction-to-Elm-elm-lang.org_.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-An-Introduction-to-Elm-elm-lang.org_.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-An-Introduction-to-Elm-elm-lang.org_-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-An-Introduction-to-Elm-elm-lang.org_-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>The official guide to Elm, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-an-introduction-to-elm-122048" target="_blank" rel="noopener">An Introduction to Elm</a>, is a <b>free </b>comprehensive resource that will teach you the basics of programming in Elm, as well as fundamental principles and patterns to help you create interactive applications using the renowned Elm Architecture. By the end, you’ll have a concrete understanding of the core ideas and patterns that make Elm nice to use.</p>
<p>Prior experience with programming languages (JavaScript preferred) is required to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll start by immediately familiarizing yourself with the values and functions of Elm. Then, you’ll quickly explore the intuitive Elm architecture by building simple buttons, text fields, and forms programs.</p>
<p>Moving on, you’ll learn about types and even create custom types yourself as a way to guarantee that your app will not crash during runtime. Pattern matching will prove itself handy when extracting values from types that hold data, or when handling errors by using Maybe and Result types.</p>
<p>The Elm Architecture handles mouse and keyboard interactions, but what about talking to servers? You’ll learn about commands and subscriptions, which are ways to handle side effects in Elm such as making HTTP requests and working with JSON data. They can also help you interoperate with JavaScript by passing data between them JavaScript.</p>
<p>Next, you&#8217;ll learn web app structure and best practices of creating web apps in concepts such as in navigation, URL Parsing, and modules. Finally, you’ll learn how to optimize an Elm app through techniques such as Html.lazy and Html.keyed for rendering large lists of data in Elm and minification for reducing the size of your code.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 12 hours long. You’ll learn by reading through the course materials and applying what you’ve learned through your own practice.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-6">6. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-elm-110591" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Elm (Exercism)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85503" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Elm-Exercism.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Elm-Exercism.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Elm-Exercism-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Elm-Exercism-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-elm-110591" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exercism</a> is a <b>free </b>platform that provides a wide range of coding exercises to help developers improve their programming skills in various different languages, one of them being Elm.</p>
<p>The best feature of Exercism is that they offer <b>free</b> personal mentoring to everyone. After completing and submitting an exercise, you can request feedback from mentors who will offer you advice on how to improve your code and think like an Elm developer.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is divided into two sections: learning mode and practice mode.</p>
<p>In learning mode, you’ll progress through a series of exercises that are designed to help you build a solid understanding of the material covered. The exercises are organized into a syllabus tree, with each concept building on the one before it.</p>
<p>The syllabus covers a wide range of topics, including Elm basics, data structures such as lists, dicts, sets, and records, and functional concepts such as partial application, function composition, and pattern matching. The exercises start with a learning exercise that explains the concept, followed by coding exercises of varying difficulty to help you solidify your understanding of the topic.</p>
<p>In practice mode, you’ll have the freedom to choose from a selection of exercises of three different levels of difficulty. If you feel confident in your abilities, you can take on more challenging exercises to test and improve your skills.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is self-paced, so you can take all the time you need to complete the 70+ hands-on programming exercises. Each exercise comes with automatic feedback of your code as well as personal mentoring to help you understand your code’s strengths and flaws.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-7">7. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/frontend-masters-advanced-elm-118047" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Advanced Elm (Frontend Masters)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85504" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Advanced-Elm-Frontend-Masters.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Advanced-Elm-Frontend-Masters.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Advanced-Elm-Frontend-Masters-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-Advanced-Elm-Frontend-Masters-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Do you want to transition from using Elm as a hobby, to using it at work or at scale? This <b>paid</b> course is for you!</p>
<p>You’ll learn the best techniques for authentication, scaling, styling, module organization, Single Page Apps, performance optimization, and much more by looking at a real-world example app called Conduit, a Medium clone.</p>
<p>Experience with JavaScript is required to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>The course begins by exploring the benefits of opaque types and validated data to help the compiler look for unhandled edge cases and prevent the codebase from compiling. You’ll also also learn about extensible data and the difference between open and closed records, and practice creating your own custom types to add constraints to your code.</p>
<p>Next, you’ll delve into organizing and scaling Elm applications as they grow in size and complexity. You’ll study another kind of type called narrowing types and how to use them to create logical boundaries, rather than relying solely on file length.</p>
<p>Reusing parts of a user interface can speed up development time and help you resolve defects. Luckily, this can be done easily with helper functions. However, there are some cases where reuse isn’t best practice, and you’ll cover those cases in the course.</p>
<p>Sometimes, there can be multiple sources of truth for the same information. You’ll learn how to ensure there is only one source of information in the end product, along with learning how to decode types.</p>
<p>Finally, you will see how everything you have learned thus far relates to building single-page applications by examining the Conduit codebase.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 4–5 hours long, and consists of eight exercises and eight lessons. After each lesson, you’ll do an exercise based on what you’ve just learned.</p>

		<title>Coursera&#8217;s New Deal with Google Could Cost the Company Millions</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-google-new-deal/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-google-new-deal/#respond</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Dhawal Shah]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Mon, 27 Feb 2023 13:47:43 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Analysis]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[News]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Coursera]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Google]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=85491</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>According to Coursera CFO, the new terms represent a significant "shift". Let's dig into the numbers.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-google-new-deal/">Coursera&#8217;s New Deal with Google Could Cost the Company Millions</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<figure id="attachment_85492" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85492" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-google-revenue-banner.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85492 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-google-revenue-banner.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-google-revenue-banner.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-google-revenue-banner-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-google-revenue-banner-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85492" class="wp-caption-text">Google&#8217;s Professional Certificates on Coursera</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Last week, Coursera published its </span><a href="https://investor.coursera.com/financials/sec-filings/sec-filings-details/default.aspx?FilingId=16429195"><span style="font-weight: 400;">2022 annual report</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I’ll post a detailed analysis soon, like <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-annual-report-10k/">I did last year</a>.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">But in this article, I’d like to focus on what Coursera’s CFO Ken Hahn described earlier this month during <a href="https://seekingalpha.com/article/4577088-coursera-inc-cour-q4-2022-earnings-call-transcript">Coursera’s earnings call</a> as a “<em>geography shift within the </em></span><em><a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/p/plstatement.asp"><span style="font-weight: 400;">P&amp;L</span></a></em><span style="font-weight: 400;">” of the company</span><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Let’s dig into it.</span></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Change</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">So what’s this “geography shift” about? Well, it stems from a significant event at Coursera: the “</span><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">multi-year contract extension we secured with our largest industry partner in this new year</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400;">”, as Hahn puts it.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This largest industry partner is Google. Basically, Google renegotiated certain terms with Coursera — in particular, their revenue share agreement. To understand the significance of the new agreement, we have to first look at the old one. Here’s how Hahn described the previous arrangement:</span></p>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">“In lieu of a higher revenue share, some industry partners prioritize additional spend to promote their brand, global reach, and social impact initiatives, which is included as part of our operating expenses, primarily as sales and marketing efforts and content production.”</span><span class="quote_deco absolute top left height-100"> </span></p>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Put simply, industry partners let Coursera get a bigger cut of the revenue generated by their offerings, and in return, Coursera invested into sales, marketing, and content production, which benefited their partners.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">For Coursera, this tradeoff had two immediate effects:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Higher margins</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: Since Coursera got a bigger cut of the revenue, their margins improved. This is particularly notable in their consumer segment.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Higher operating expenses</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: Since Coursera invested more in sales, marketing, and content production, their operating expenses increased.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I was able to verify this to a certain point by looking at Coursera’s segment margin and losses over the years. I came across these during my analysis of their </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-s1-analysis/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">IPO filing (S–1)</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-annual-report-10k/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">2021 annual report (10–K)</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<div class="table">
<table>
<caption style="caption-side: bottom;">Gross margin over the years: segments &amp; total</caption>
<thead>
<tr>
<td></td>
<td><b>Consumer Margin</b></td>

<td><b>Total Margin</b></td>
</tr>

</tr>

<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">52%</span></td>
<td></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">52%</span></td>
</tr>

</table>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Here’s how Coursera defines the Segment (Consumer, Enterprise, and Degrees) Gross Margin:</span></p>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Segment gross profit represents segment revenue less content costs paid to educator partners; segment gross margin is the quotient of segment gross profit and segment revenue.</span><span class="quote_deco absolute top left height-100"> </span></p>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google’s first </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/microcredentials/coursera-professional-certificate"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Professional Certificate</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> on Coursera, the </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/google-it-support-18565"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google IT Support Certificate</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, was announced back in 2018. But it was only in March 2021 that Google introduced three new certificates on the platform. As you can see above, in 2021, Coursera’s consumer margin jumped to 66%, from 55% the prior year.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">And in Q2 2021, Coursera’s losses increased significantly, from 18.7M to 46.4M, as you can see below.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-quarterly-losses-2020-2022.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85528" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-quarterly-losses-2020-2022.png" alt="Coursera Quarterly Losses Graph" width="1666" height="1024" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-quarterly-losses-2020-2022.png 1666w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-quarterly-losses-2020-2022-300x184.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-quarterly-losses-2020-2022-1024x629.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-quarterly-losses-2020-2022-768x472.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/coursera-quarterly-losses-2020-2022-1536x944.png 1536w" sizes="(max-width: 1666px) 100vw, 1666px" /></a></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">So the expansion of Google’s offering coincided with a higher consumer margin and higher losses on Coursera’s side. This seems consistent with Hahn’s description of their prior agreement, suggesting that the losses might stem from the additional “<em>sales and marketing efforts and content production</em>”.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Those were the old terms. Now, let’s look at the new ones.</span></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">The Impact</span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Under the new terms, Google and Coursera are switching to a more “standard revenue share”. And this transition is what is supposed to bring about the “geography shift” discussed earlier. Here’s how the CFO put it in the earnings call:</span></p>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">“First, the transition to a more standard revenue share will result in a geography shift within the P&amp;L of an estimated 10 percentage points of total revenue, from operating expense to cost of revenue. </span><b>We now expect both total gross margin and our Consumer segment margin to be approximately 52% this year</b>.”<span class="quote_deco absolute top left height-100"> </span></p>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-annual-report-10k/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Coursera’s 2021 annual report (10–K)</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, the “cost of revenue” is defined as follows:</span></p>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">“Cost of revenue consists of content costs in the form of a fee paid to educator partners and expenses associated with the operation and maintenance of the Company’s platform. These expenses include the cost of servicing both paid learner and educator partner support requests, hosting and bandwidth costs, amortization of acquired technology and internal-use software, customer payment processing fees, and allocated depreciation and facilities costs.”</span><span class="quote_deco absolute top left height-100"> </span></p>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">But I think in this case, it’s mainly the content costs, in the form of a fee paid to partners. Per Coursera’s annual report, other expenses don’t seem to be factored into segment margins:</span></p>
<div class="quote relative padding-horz-large xlarge-up-padding-horz-xxlarge padding-vert-xxsmall margin-bottom-large quote-pull quote-text">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">“Expenses other than content costs included in cost of revenue are not allocated to segments because they are managed at the consolidated corporate level.”</span><span class="quote_deco absolute top left height-100"> </span></p>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In other words, Google will now take a bigger cut of the revenue generated by its offerings. But Coursera won’t be required to invest as much into sales and marketing. So for Coursera, content costs go up, but the operation expenses go down. This is the “geography shift” Hahn was talking about.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">But for 2023, the Coursera CFO expects the company to “incur expenses of $25 million in 2023, which will be similar in nature to our historic spend for the program, including sales and marketing efforts, content production, and product development.”</span></p>
<h2><span style="font-weight: 400;">Google’s Share of Coursera’s Revenue </span></h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">So this begs the question: how much revenue does Google contribute to Coursera?</span></p>
<div class="table">
<table>
<caption style="caption-side: bottom;">Coursera: margin &amp; profit</caption>
<thead>
<tr>
<td></td>
<td><b>2022</b></td>
<td><b>2023</b></td>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><b>Total Revenue</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">$523M</span></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">$600M</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><b>Gross Margin</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">63%</span></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">52%</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><b>Gross Profit</b></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">$329M</span></td>
<td><span style="font-weight: 400;">$312M</span></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In 2023, Coursera expects revenue in the $595–605 million range, up from $523 million in 2022, which represents an increase of about 15%. But despite this growth, Coursera expects its 2023 gross profit to be less than in 2022. This is largely due to Coursera&#8217;s new contract with Google.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If the new terms between Coursera and Google had come into effect a year earlier — that is, if the gross margin in 2022 had been 52% — Coursera’s gross profit in 2022 would have been $272M. That’s $57M less than what they actually made. So, can we assume that all this money is going to Google?</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In addition, we also know from Coursera’s annual report that “30% of our total revenue comes from the content and credentialing programs of five partners”. So for 2022 this amounts to $157 million.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This puts Google’s revenue in the $57–157 million range. Therefore, it’s quite possible that Coursera makes around $100M from Google courses. The new terms impact Coursera’s margin on this revenue, hence the “geography shift”.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">To learn more about the business side of Coursera, read our previous coverage:</span></p>

<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-beats-udemy-b2c/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Content vs Credential: Coursera Beats Udemy’s B2C Revenue</span></a></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/coursera-layoffs/"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Coursera Conducts Layoffs to “Slow our Rate of Spending”</span></a></li>
</ul>

		<title>Rethinking Happiness to Increase Our Well-Being</title>
		<link>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-science-of-well-being/</link>
					<comments>https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-science-of-well-being/#respond</comments>
		
		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Kohei Iwahara]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Tue, 21 Feb 2023 18:12:03 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Reviews]]></category>
		<guid isPermaLink="false">https://www.classcentral.com/report/?p=85398</guid>

					<description><![CDATA[<p>This is an in-depth review of The Science of Well-Being course by Yale University with Professor Laurie Santos.</p>
<p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/review-science-of-well-being/">Rethinking Happiness to Increase Our Well-Being</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p>
]]></description>
										<content:encoded><![CDATA[<figure id="attachment_85399" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85399" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85399" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Instructor-Professor-Laurie-Santos.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Instructor-Professor-Laurie-Santos.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Instructor-Professor-Laurie-Santos-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Instructor-Professor-Laurie-Santos-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85399" class="wp-caption-text">Professor Laurie Santos, course instructor.</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/the-science-of-well-being-10346" target="_blank" rel="noopener">The Science of Well-Being</a>, offered by <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/university/yale" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Yale University</a> on Coursera, is an insightful course introducing practices to increase our well-being. Like most of us, my lifestyle significantly changed at the height of the pandemic. By spending most of the day at my apartment alone for months, I gradually began to question my personal values on happiness and wondered how I can increase my sense of fulfillment. So, I decided to enroll in this 10-week course, hoping that I can learn some insights to improve my well-being.</p>
<p>This course has also been featured in:</p>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/most-popular-online-courses/">[2023] The 250 Most Popular Online Courses of All Time</a></li>
<li aria-level="1"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/top-moocs-2022-edition/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Class Central’s Best Online Courses of All Time (2022 Edition)</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Understanding What Makes Us Happy</h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85400" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Although we generally believe that a good job, awesome stuff, or true love will make ourselves happy, psychologists advocate that this is an illusion. Professor Laurie Santos argues that they stop bringing you the happiness you expect and rest your reference point for the future, because you habituate with your high salary, fancy car, and partner. Throughout the course, she discusses why we have such misconceptions about happiness and how we can overcome our biases. After introducing what really increases our well-being, Professor Santos suggests strategies to develop habits to put them into practice. The encouraging finding in psychology is that we can work forward to improve our well-being, because actions and thoughts control 40% of our happiness.</p>
<p>For sure, some of the recommended rewirements, practices to increase our happiness, were rather common sense. I knew from my experiences that regular physical exercise, meditation, and good sleep improve my well-being. Still, what was interesting with this course is that all the suggestions were based on evidence from psychological research. For example, academic research using a brain scanner has shown that meditation not only increases your happiness via shutting off the default mode of mind wandering but also strengthens our brain over time. These empirical research findings increase my confidence and motivation to put them into practice.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85402" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-3.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-3.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-3-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-3-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>On the other hand, some of the findings were counter intuitive. For example, investments on experiences will make you happier than purchasing materials. My intuition was that material possessions such as a fancy new car will continue to bring happiness in the future. However, Professor Santos argued that while we habituate to a new car, a nice vacation will end well before we get used to it. In fact, when I recall my good memories in the past, vacations, especially the ones I spent with my family or friends, came on top of my list and certainly not the things I purchased for myself.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85401" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-2.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-2.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-2-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-2-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Furthermore, Professor Santos gave a fresh perspective on what can make you call a dream job. Instead of seeking high salaries, we should look for jobs that actively use our signature strengths, character strengths most essential to who we are. The act of using those strengths raises our happiness and lowers depressive symptoms, which in turn increases our productivity and job satisfaction. In fact, a good understanding of my signature strengths after taking a free self-assessment introduced in the course certainly gave me a new and interesting angle on how to approach my work differently.</p>
<h2>Practicing What Makes Us Happy</h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85403" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-4.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-4.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-4-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/The-Science-of-Well-Being-Yale-Concepts-4-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>The last four weeks were devoted to practicing our favorite rewirement taught in the course. While I chose signature strength, my challenge was to practice it every day, which became apparent during the last week on the project. The positive momentum and enthusiasm can fade surprisingly quickly. I ended up procrastinating, which took me much longer to complete the Rewirement Challenge. This experience revealed that merely knowing something is not enough to put them into practice, which was referred to as the GI Joe fallacy in the first week of this course.</p>
<p>The important lesson was to have strategies for better habits, which was introduced in the sixth week. What I found interesting is that we need to think about the benefits and obstacles of our goal beforehand, if we want to keep overcoming obstacles. My tendency has been either optimistic without considering obstacles, or pessimistic focusing on obstacles, which have limited my potential. Furthermore, we should create beforehand implementation intentions and very specific if-then plans to respond to obstacles, so that we achieve our goal.</p>
<h2>Conclusion</h2>
<p>Overall, I really enjoyed this 10-week course. The teaching style was very engaging, full of insightful material, which helped me rethink what makes me happy. The recommended reading on signature strength was eye-opening, giving me the courage to confront the root causes of my personal problems and to find solutions for them. Because this course introduces many rewirements to improve your well-being, I am sure you can find something that would meet your preferences. Above all, my happiness score improved over the course. Highly recommended!</p>
<figure id="attachment_85404" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85404" style="width: 697px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85404" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Kohei-Iwahara-Certificate.png" alt="" width="697" height="538" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Kohei-Iwahara-Certificate.png 697w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Kohei-Iwahara-Certificate-300x232.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 697px) 100vw, 697px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85404" class="wp-caption-text">My certificate of completion.</figcaption></figure>

<h2>What is Resume Writing?</h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">A resume is a formal document, typically of one to two pages, that highlights a candidate’s education, experience and skills. Job seekers write resumes while applying for a job for recruiters to evaluate their competency and worth for the concerned job. Employers may collect resumes in person, through a company&#8217;s career website, a job search engine, or a professional social media page.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The word “resume” originally comes from the French word ‘</span><a href="https://www.merriam-webster.com/dictionary/resume#word-history" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">résumé</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">’, past participle of résumer which means “to summarize”. However, this term is primarily used in America and Canada to represent a document that showcases your skills and work experiences, and not in France and other parts of Europe where a curriculum vitae (or CV) is used instead. In India, Pakistan and Bangladesh, biodata is often used in place of a resume.</span></p>
<p><b>Fun fact</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">: Did you know that Leonardo da Vinci was the first recorded person to write a resume in the 15th century (even though it was more of a letter)?</span></p>
<figure id="attachment_85458" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85458" style="width: 526px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85458" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Leonardo-da-Vinci-Resume.png" alt="" width="526" height="686" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Leonardo-da-Vinci-Resume.png 526w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/Leonardo-da-Vinci-Resume-230x300.png 230w" sizes="(max-width: 526px) 100vw, 526px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85458" class="wp-caption-text">Leonardo’s “resume” (image credit: <a href="https://www.davron.net/history-of-the-resume/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">DAVRON</a>)</figcaption></figure>
<h3>Why are Resume Writing Skills Important?</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Resumes create your first impression to potential employers. That’s why resume writing is an important skill to have. </span><a href="https://www.indeed.com/career-advice/resumes-cover-letters/what-is-a-resume" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Indeed</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> notes down a few more reasons why resumes are important:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Provides an opportunity to market yourself to employers</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Outlines your skills, background and education so employers can easily see how your experience contributes to the success of a company</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Helps employers eliminate unqualified candidates</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Allows you to demonstrate your written communication skills</span></li>
</ul>
<h3>What is My Experience with Resume Writing?</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Throughout school and college, I was taught to write good resumes as part of my curriculum and I scored high too. And I landed a pretty decent job alright!</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Besides that, I am a </span><a href="https://www.coursera.org/instructor/archisha-bhar" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Guided Project Instructor</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and a Beta Tester at Coursera, having tested many courses before they’re officially launched. I have taken </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">over 50 online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> in various subjects.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My experience as an online learner and teacher has given me some perspective on what to look for in an online course. I used my experience to evaluate each course in this list.</span></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79248 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png" alt="Find your next course on Class Central" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-2-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2>Course Ranking Methodology</h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology I used in previous rankings (</span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">you can find them all here</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">). It involves a three-step process:</span></p>
<ol>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">100K online courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/resume-writing" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">50+ resume writing courses</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@archisha" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span style="font-weight: 400;">learner</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, release date, affordability, ratings and enrollments.</span></li>
</ol>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The end result is a unique selection of courses that combines a decade of Class Central data and my own experience as an online learner to try to get the best of both worlds. So far, I’ve spent more than 10 hours building this list, and I’ll continue to update it.</span></p>
<h2>Course Ranking Statistics</h2>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Here are some statistics regarding this course ranking:</span></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Combined, these courses have accrued over </span><b>760.6K</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> enrollments.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">3 courses are </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> or </span><b>free-to-audit</b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> and 7 courses are </span><b>paid</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">The most-represented course provider in the ranking is </span><b>LinkedIn Learning</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">, with 4 courses.</span></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">All 10 courses are in English.</span></li>

<h2 id="anchor-1">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-writing-a-resume-31652" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Writing a Resume (LinkedIn Learning)</a></h2>
<figure id="attachment_85448" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85448" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85448" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Writing-a-Resume-LinkedIn-Learning.png" alt="" width="1536" height="768" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Writing-a-Resume-LinkedIn-Learning.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Writing-a-Resume-LinkedIn-Learning-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Writing-a-Resume-LinkedIn-Learning-1024x512.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-Writing-a-Resume-LinkedIn-Learning-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85448" class="wp-caption-text">Stacey Gordon, instructor</figcaption></figure>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My first pick for the best resume writing online course is the </span><b>free course</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-writing-a-resume-31652" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Writing a Resume</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> on LinkedIn Learning.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This </span><b>free</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">, beginner-friendly course will teach you the basics of resume writing. What’s more – as a job-seeker, you’ll also understand a few extra job search basics such as identifying companies to work for and determining fit. Moreover, you’ll be able to tackle job hopping, lack of experience, or unemployment gaps while focusing on your experiences.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">By the end of the course, you’ll learn what to and what not to include in your resume and showcase your talents and best qualities. You’ll be able to choose the right format for your resume, tailor information to match job requirements, and write alternative resumes that include industry-specific information.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">First, you’ll learn how to create an effective resume by understanding its basic components such as the objective statement, skills section, work experience, education, and technical skills. You&#8217;ll customize these components to match the job you&#8217;re applying for, upgrade your resume by using achievements, awards, and publications, and choose the right layout and formatting.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Next, you’ll cover alternative resume designs, including resumes for different industries and regions, and how to handle common challenges like career changes, gaps in employment, and long-term unemployment.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">After that, you&#8217;ll understand how to use your resume to stand out from other applicants and conduct a successful job search by focusing on your objective, showcasing the skills that employers want, and effectively using your education and volunteer work.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Finally, you&#8217;ll also learn best practices for using a resume in various scenarios, such as online applications, interviews, networking, and informational interviews, and conduct a proactive versus reactive job search by identifying potential companies, determining fit, and finding contacts.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 10 modules. Each module involves about 10 to 20 minutes of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, practice exercises and quizzes.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My second pick for the best resume writing online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/winning-resumes-5477" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Writing Winning Resumes and Cover Letters</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by the University of Maryland, College Park on Coursera.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This course is for intermediate learners who want to grab the attention of prospective employers using the language they already speak inside their organization. You’ll get answers to any related questions that you might have, and convert a boring resume into a dynamic asset statement. By the end of this course, you’ll be able to write your resume in a language that employers understand.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn how to tailor your resume for a specific job opportunity and to rank high in the relevance scales used by top organizations, and craft powerful accomplishment statements and summarize your experiences effectively.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll also select the best resume format for your career goals, prepare your resume for electronic submission, and write an effective cover letter. You’ll also cover what information to leave off your resume and how to follow up after an interview.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 4 weeks. Each week involves about 3 to 4 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My third pick for the best resume writing online course is the </span><b>free-to-audit</b> <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/how-to-write-a-resume-5830" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">How to Write a Resume (Project-Centered Course)</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;">, offered by the State University of New York on &lt;provider&gt;.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">If you’re a young professional or a college student, then this resume writing course is for you. Whether it’s your first resume or an old resume you want to polish, this project-based course will teach you resume best practices and current trends. Regardless of your career stage or professional background, you can benefit from this course and learn by working on a real-world project.</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll learn about the purpose of a resume and when it might be used, examine the typical sections of a resume, identify transferable skills from your past experiences, write effective action-statements, use strong verbs, and avoid common pitfalls in writing the content of your resume.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll also organize the sections and create a clear and structured format, become familiar with different headings and &#8220;buzzwords&#8221;, take a look at an interview with an employer that will provide valuable insights to make your resume stand out, and get answers to any common questions you may have about resumes.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 7 weeks. Each week involves about 30 minutes to 2 hours of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos, readings and quizzes.</span></p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">My fourth pick for the best resume writing online course is </span><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/linkedin-learning-writing-a-tech-resume-31653" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><i><span style="font-weight: 400;">Writing a Tech Resume</span></i></a><span style="font-weight: 400;"> on LinkedIn Learning.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Focused on those from a technical background, this course shows you how to showcase your technology skills so that you can stand out from the crowd. You’ll work on minor design details like spacing, font choice and color palette, and create your professional online presence on platforms such as LinkedIn and GitHub. And you can achieve all this in less than an hour!</span></p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">In this course, you’ll cover everything from logistics, such as resume length and the difference between a resume and a CV, to content tips and tricks, like word choice and highlighting your impact.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">You’ll learn what to include in your resume, such as education, work experience, skills, and awards and certifications, as well as how to use tools like word processors, resume builders, and visual design tools to create a polished and professional final product.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">Finally, you’ll understand design best practices, such as typography, color, layout, and file format, and how to present a professional online presence through platforms like LinkedIn, GitHub and personal portfolios or websites.</span></p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">The course is broken down into 7 modules. Each module involves about 5 to 10 minutes of work. Concepts are taught through a combination of videos and quizzes.</span></p>

<p>In this guide, you will find the best free online courses and resources to learn OCaml,  a general-purpose, statically-typed programming language that is widely used for building robust, expressive, and performant applications.</p>
<p>Though OCaml puts the functional style first, it supports other paradigms like object-oriented and imperative programming, giving developers a high degree of flexibility. Along with its robust type system which guarantees safety and reliability, OCaml is a popular choice among large organizations such as Facebook, Microsoft, Bloomberg, and Jane Street. OCaml&#8217;s versatile nature enables developers to use it for a wide range of tasks, from writing compilers and developing trading systems, to creating domain-specific languages and web-crawling applications.</p>
<p>If you’re interested in learning a language that combines efficiency, expressiveness, and practicality in a way unmatched by any other language, read on more to find my top picks for the best OCaml course.</p>

<h2>What is OCaml?</h2>
<p>OCaml is a general-purpose, statically-typed programming language with an emphasis on expressiveness and safety. It was designed in 1996 by Xavier Leroy and his team at INRIA in France as an extension of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ML_(programming_language)" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Meta Language</a> Caml dialect. Although Caml had a powerful type system and functional programming capabilities, it was only ever used in academia. However, by incorporating features such as object-oriented programming while retaining the correctness and conciseness of its predecessor, OCaml became a suitable language for building practical, real-world applications (which is what the O in OCaml formerly stood for Objective, if you were wondering).</p>
<p>OCaml&#8217;s strong type system, inherited from its predecessors, helps ensure code is safe and correct by catching errors at compile-time, while maintaining the flexibility of untyped languages by performing type inference. Not only that, OCaml’s algebraic data types allows for powerful pattern-matching capabilities, making it easy to match, extract and manipulate data in a concise and expressive way.</p>
<p>Many of OCaml’s features encourage programming in the functional style, such as preferring recursion and higher-order functions over traditional loops and preferring immutable data structures over mutable ones. However, it acknowledges that certain tasks  such as working with files and writing in-place algorithms can be difficult to accomplish using only functional methods. As a result, OCaml offers support for multiple programming paradigms like imperative and object-oriented programming, giving developers flexibility to choose the best paradigm for their problem.</p>
<p>OCaml is also known for performance and ability to easily integrate with other languages, such as C and JavaScript, making it a great choice for building multi-language systems.</p>
<p>As for its applications, OCaml is widely used in academia and research institutions, with many universities like Cornell and Princeton including it in their curriculum to teach functional programming. And although OCaml is relatively niche compared to other languages, it has been used in <a href="https://ocaml.org/industrial-users" target="_blank" rel="noopener">several large-scale industry projects</a> by companies such as Facebook for compilers and static analysis, Jane Street for guaranteeing the correctness of their internal trading systems, Coq for checking mathematical theorems, and Bloomberg for advanced financial derivatives risk management application.<br />
<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p>
<h2>Best Courses Guides Methodology</h2>
<p>I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). It involves a three-step process:</p>
<ol>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Research:</b> I started by leveraging Class Central’s database with <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subjects" target="_blank" rel="noopener">100K online courses</a> and 200K+ reviews. Then, I made a preliminary selection of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/subject/ocaml" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OCaml courses</a> by rating, reviews, and bookmarks.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Evaluate:</b> I read through reviews on Class Central, Reddit, and course providers to understand what other learners thought about each course and combined it with my own experience as a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/@Elham" target="_blank" rel="noopener">learner</a>.</li>
<li aria-level="1"><b>Select:</b> Well-made courses were picked if they presented valuable and engaging content and they have to fit in a set of criteria and be ranked accordingly: comprehensive curriculum, affordability, release date, ratings and enrollments.</li>
</ol>

<p>Here are some aggregate stats about the ranking:</p>
<ul>

<li aria-level="1">All of the courses are suitable for beginners to OCaml. Unfortunately, none of the courses are geared towards complete beginners to programming.</li>

<p>Without further ado, let’s go through the top picks.</p>
<h2 id="anchor-1">1. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-ocaml-programming-correct-efficient-beautiful-121110" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OCaml Programming: Correct + Efficient + Beautiful  (Cornell University)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85426" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-OCaml-Programming_-Correct-Efficient-Beautiful-Cornell-University.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-OCaml-Programming_-Correct-Efficient-Beautiful-Cornell-University.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-OCaml-Programming_-Correct-Efficient-Beautiful-Cornell-University-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/1.-OCaml-Programming_-Correct-Efficient-Beautiful-Cornell-University-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>The number one OCaml course in this ranking is <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-ocaml-programming-correct-efficient-beautiful-121110" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OCaml Programming: Correct + Efficient + Beautiful</a> from Cornell University.</p>
<p>This <b>free</b> course is my top pick because it is both a textbook and a bite-sized video series. This means that you’ll learn not only through comprehensive written explanations and examples, but also through visual demonstrations and coding exercises.</p>
<p>The course covers a wide range of topics related to OCaml, including functional programming, correctness and efficiency, data structures, and best software engineering practices.</p>
<p>Prior knowledge programming in some mainstream imperative language (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-java-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Java</a> and <a href="https://www.freecodecamp.org/news/best-python-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Python</a> preferred) and first-semester standard discrete mathematics is assumed prior to taking this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll start straight away by diving into the basics of OCaml, starting with basic syntax like writing expressions and functions. You’ll quickly familiarize yourself with the functional style of programming through extensive use of OCaml’s REPL.</p>
<p>As you become more comfortable with the language’s distinctive syntax, you’ll find yourself appreciating its underlying principles that help developers write concise yet expressive, correct yet efficient code. For example, OCaml is awesome for <a href="http://ocamlverse.net/content/compilers.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">writing compilers</a> thanks to functional programming concepts such as parametric polymorphism, algebraic data types, higher-order programming, pattern matching. Hence, you’ll study all of these in-depth, along software engineering best practices such as error handling, testing, and documentation.</p>
<p>Not only that, data structures will also be covered in the course, from the ones available in the standard library to more complicated data structures that you’ll implement on your own using both imperative and functional programming. You’ll be able to analyze the efficiency of data structures using amortized analysis and choose the one that suits your use case.</p>
<p>Remember that I mentioned OCaml is great for writing compilers? Well, the final part of this course demystifies compilers enough for you to design and implement some small, special-purpose domain-specific languages (DSLs).</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course consists of 9 chapters. You’ll learn by reading through the chapters and watching the videos. At the end of each chapter except the first, you’ll find exercises for you to practice what you’ve learned. Additionally, the course has a feature called collaborative annotations that allows you to highlight and make private notes that you can share with others.</p>

Due to overwhelming positive feedback, Michael made the videos publicly available for anyone who wants to learn about OCaml, functional programming, and becoming a better programmer.</li>

<h2 id="anchor-2">2. <a href="https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLGC2in6hSHQcmT_cz4t7ePeQtTCkNkvll" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Functional Programming in OCaml (Université Paris Diderot)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85432" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Introduction-to-Functional-Programming-in-OCaml-Universite-Paris-Diderot.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Introduction-to-Functional-Programming-in-OCaml-Universite-Paris-Diderot.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Introduction-to-Functional-Programming-in-OCaml-Universite-Paris-Diderot-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/2.-Introduction-to-Functional-Programming-in-OCaml-Universite-Paris-Diderot-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>My second pick for the best OCaml course is <a href="https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLGC2in6hSHQcmT_cz4t7ePeQtTCkNkvll" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Introduction to Functional Programming in OCaml</a> offered by Université de Paris.</p>
<p>This MOOC focuses on teaching the principles of functional programming using the OCaml programming language by emphasizing the use of functions as first-class values to create and manage complex data structures. The course will begin by showing the use of OCaml as a functional programming language alone, and by the end, it’ll demonstrate how OCaml can be utilized as a multi-paradigm language, combining functional and imperative programming styles to get the best of both worlds.</p>
<p>To follow this course, you should already have some basic knowledge of writing simple computer programs in a programming language.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll begin the course with an overview of the language, starting with its robust type system. OCaml is statically-typed language, but thanks to its flexible type inference you’ll find yourself working with the type-checker rather than against it, and even create your own types. Combined with immutable data structures, such as tuples, records, and trees, you’ll see how they can be used effectively in your programs.</p>
<p>As a functional-first programming language, OCaml emphasizes the concepts of functional programming (FP), including the use of recursion over loops and the treatment of functions as first-class citizens. You’ll gain hands-on experience with key FP concepts such as partial function application, map and fold operations, and more.</p>
<p>By now, you’ve probably gotten a good understanding of how functional programming differs from imperative programming. Imperative programming is useful in some cases though, so you’ll explore OCaml’s imperative constructs such as modules, input/output, and exceptions.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 6 weeks long, with the total video watch time adding up to 7 hours. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos and following along with the examples provided by the instructors.</p>

<h3>Fun Facts</h3>
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Roberto Di Cosmo is professor of computer science at University Paris Diderot, director of Irill, currently on leave at INRIA. His research interests include functional and parallel programming, type systems, logic, rewriting, and the static analysis of large software collections.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Yann Régis-Gianas teaches computer science at Université Paris-Diderot. His research at the PPS laboratory focuses on the theory and the design of programming languages. He did his PhD in the INRIA team that develops OCaml and is now in the development team of the Coq proof assistant.</li>
<li aria-level="1">Ralf Treinen is professor of computer science at University Paris Diderot. Symbolic constraint solving, verification and application of formal methods to the quality assurance of software components are among his current research interests. He is also a member of Irill.</li>
</ul>
<p>If you&#8217;re interested in this course, you can find <a href="https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLGC2in6hSHQcmT_cz4t7ePeQtTCkNkvll" target="_blank" rel="noopener">more information about the course and how to enroll here</a>.</p>
<h2 id="anchor-3">3. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-programming-with-ocaml-122060" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Programming with OCaml (Anthony Narlock)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85431" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Programming-with-OCaml-Anthony-Narlock.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Programming-with-OCaml-Anthony-Narlock.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Programming-with-OCaml-Anthony-Narlock-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/3.-Programming-with-OCaml-Anthony-Narlock-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/youtube-programming-with-ocaml-122060" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Programming with OCaml</a> teaches the basics of programming in OCaml, especially how it differs from other traditional programming languages.</p>
<p>No prior knowledge of OCaml is required to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll start this course by getting familiar with the command line tool `utop`. You&#8217;ll explore OCaml&#8217;s powerful static type system, including its basic types such as integers, floats, booleans, strings, and characters. Additionally, you&#8217;ll be introduced to the concepts of recursion and higher-order functions, and understand why they&#8217;re often preferred over loops.</p>
<p>As you move on, you&#8217;ll delve into lists and pattern matching. You&#8217;ll learn how to create and add elements to lists in OCaml, and discover how they can be composed of different types using tuples. You&#8217;ll see the power of lists and tuples through practical examples of pattern matching.</p>
<p>Taking a step back, you’ll delve into higher-order functions, focusing on the functions that operate on lists such as List.map, List.filter, List.fold_left, and List.fold_right.</p>
<p>Finally, the course will cover advanced concepts like parametric polymorphism, which allows types with free variables to be replaced with any type, and inductive types, which are programmer-defined types created using the &#8220;type&#8221; keyword in OCaml. You&#8217;ll see an example of this by creating a &#8220;message&#8221; type with different constructors for string, bool, and float messages, and then defining a list of message types and writing a function that iterates over them.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is 3–4 hours long. You’ll learn by watching the lecture videos, where you’ll see the instructor teaching the basics of the language as well as complete some practical exercises to recap what you’ve learned in the video.</p>

He has a YouTube channel where he posts study with me, vlogs, educational tutorials, and software update videos.</li>

<h2 id="anchor-4">4. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-ocaml-by-examples-121112" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OCaml By Example (O(1) Labs)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85427" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-OCaml-By-Example-O1-Labs.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-OCaml-By-Example-O1-Labs.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-OCaml-By-Example-O1-Labs-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/4.-OCaml-By-Example-O1-Labs-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>Learn the OCaml language by following a series of examples in the <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-ocaml-by-examples-121112" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ocaml By Example course</a>!</p>
<p>No prior experience of OCaml is required to take this course.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll start this course with an overview of the basic language constructs such as values, functions, pattern matching, tuples, variants, lists, sets, arrays, and records. Although most of the concepts you’ll learn relate to functional programming, you’ll also understand how to program imperatively in OCaml as it is a multi-paradigm language.</p>
<p>Next, you’ll study data structures and algorithms, such as recursion, hash tables, and their implementation in the OCaml language. You’ll also understand the different ways to organize your code, such as modules and packages with the Dune build tool. Error handling and interacting with the file system are some other concepts you’ll also cover.</p>
<p>Finally, you’ll learn the more advanced parts of Ocaml, such as macros, and explore OCaml’s vast library collection, including interoperating with other programming languages such as C, JavaScript, and Rust.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is made up of four chapters. You’ll learn by reading through the different articles along with the code examples provided.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-5">5. <a href="https://github.com/janestreet/learn-ocaml-workshop" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OCaml Workshop (Jane Street)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85428" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-OCaml-Workshop-Jane-Street.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-OCaml-Workshop-Jane-Street.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-OCaml-Workshop-Jane-Street-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/5.-OCaml-Workshop-Jane-Street-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://github.com/janestreet/learn-ocaml-workshop" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Jane Street’s OCaml Workshop</a> aims to help people start developing in OCaml through small hands-on exercises and bigger, more complex projects like arcade games.</p>
<p>To take this workshop, you should have some experience with OCaml.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>After you get familiarized with OCaml’s build process and tools, you’ll complete twenty one exercises teaching you OCaml features such as pattern matching, higher order functions, options, and anonymous functions.</p>
<p>Once you get that covered, you’ll begin developing simplified clones of three arcade games: Snake, Lumines, and Frogger. Snake and Lumines both run on your computer, whereas Frogger runs on your web browser. Afterward, you can choose between several more advanced projects, such as writing a IRC bot, implementing <a href="https://github.com/junegunn/fzf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">command-line fuzzy finder</a>, or improving Frogger.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>Two types of exercises are given: small coding exercises and large projects. Small coding exercises test your understanding of different programming aspects of the OCaml language, whereas the larger projects provide the opportunity to apply your knowledge and skills to more complex, real-world problems. You’ll need to pass the `expect` tests in order to fully complete the exercises.</p>
<p>The course also provides a few paths you can take after completing the exercises, but these come without `expect` tests.</p>

<li aria-level="1">This workshop was part of the The OCaml Users and Developers Workshop that brings together the OCaml community, including users of OCaml in industry, academia, hobbyists, and the free software community.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anchor-6">6. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-learn-ocaml-121114" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn OCaml (OCaml Software Foundation)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85429" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Learn-OCaml-OCaml-Software-Foundation.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Learn-OCaml-OCaml-Software-Foundation.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Learn-OCaml-OCaml-Software-Foundation-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/6.-Learn-OCaml-OCaml-Software-Foundation-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p>OCaml Software Foundation’s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/independent-learn-ocaml-121114" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Learn OCaml</a> site provides a variety of coding challenges for you to practice OCaml programming taken from Université de Paris OCaml courses.</p>
<p>Experience with OCaml is recommended to do the exercises.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>The difficulty of the exercises ranges from one star (very easy) to four stars (very hard).</p>
<p>Some of the easier exercises include searching for strings in arrays, balancing binary trees, and using first-class functions.</p>
<p>Meanwhile, the more difficult exercises include implementing algorithms such as merge sort and huffman compression, displaying a filesystem hierarchy, and developing a mini database.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>You’ll write and execute code directly in the browser’s coding environment. After each exercise, you’ll receive a grade based on how efficient your code is.</p>

<h2 id="anchor-7">7. <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-ocaml-110604" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OCaml (Exercism)</a></h2>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-85430" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-OCaml-Exercism.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-OCaml-Exercism.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-OCaml-Exercism-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/7.-OCaml-Exercism-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p>
<p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/exercism-ocaml-110604" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Exercism</a> is an online coding platform that offers a variety of programming exercises and challenges that are suitable for all skill levels. It&#8217;s a great way to practice and improve your OCaml coding skills for <b>free</b>.</p>
<p>What makes Exercism stand out from other similar exercise providers is that it offers a <b>free </b>mentoring service. If you ever get stuck on an exercise or want to improve your code, you can request feedback from experienced OCaml programmers.</p>
<h3>What You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>Exercism offers exercises of varying difficulty levels, including easy, medium, and hard.</p>
<p>Examples of easy exercises include reporting leap years, calculating ages of people in a planet’s solar years, and determining if a sentence is a pangram.</p>
<p>Medium exercises include tasks such as counting the number of rectangles in an ASCII diagram, scoring a bowling game, and adding numbers to a minesweeper board.</p>
<p>For those looking for more of a challenge, there are also hard exercises available, such as calculating the date of meetups, implementing logic of hangman game using functional reactive programming, and creating a zipper for a binary tree.</p>
<h3>How You’ll Learn</h3>
<p>This course is self-paced, so you can take all the time you need to complete the 40+ hands-on programming exercises. Each exercise comes with automatic feedback of your code as well as personal mentoring to help you understand your code’s strengths and flaws.</p>

		<dc:creator><![CDATA[Dhawal Shah]]></dc:creator>
		<pubDate>Mon, 20 Feb 2023 13:45:48 +0000</pubDate>
				<category><![CDATA[Guides]]></category>
